\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Telements_8h_source_l00994}00994       \textcolor{comment}{// The appropriate amount of the cubic bubble function is}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Telements_8h_source_l00997}00997 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Telements_8h_source_l00998}00998       \textcolor{comment}{// note that s[2] needs replacing by s\_2 everywhere since only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Telements_8h_source_l00999}00999       \textcolor{comment}{// two independent variables s[0],s[1] and s\_2 is expressed in terms of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Telements_8h_source_l01000}01000       \textcolor{comment}{// those later.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Telements_8h_source_l01001}01001       psi[0] = 2.0 * \mbox{\hyperlink{cfortran_8h_ab7123126e4885ef647dd9c6e3807a21c}{s}}[0] * (\mbox{\hyperlink{cfortran_8h_ab7123126e4885ef647dd9c6e3807a21c}{s}}[0] -\/ 0.5) + 3.0 * cubic\_bubble;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Telements_8h_source_l01002}01002       psi[1] = 2.0 * \mbox{\hyperlink{cfortran_8h_ab7123126e4885ef647dd9c6e3807a21c}{s}}[1] * (\mbox{\hyperlink{cfortran_8h_ab7123126e4885ef647dd9c6e3807a21c}{s}}[1] -\/ 0.5) + 3.0 * cubic\_bubble;}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Telements_8h_source_l01004}01004       psi[3] = 4.0 * \mbox{\hyperlink{cfortran_8h_ab7123126e4885ef647dd9c6e3807a21c}{s}}[0] * \mbox{\hyperlink{cfortran_8h_ab7123126e4885ef647dd9c6e3807a21c}{s}}[1] -\/ 12.0 * cubic\_bubble;}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Telements_8h_source_l01006}01006       psi[5] = 4.0 * s\_2 * \mbox{\hyperlink{cfortran_8h_ab7123126e4885ef647dd9c6e3807a21c}{s}}[0] -\/ 12.0 * cubic\_bubble;}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Telements_8h_source_l01804}01804                 \mbox{\hyperlink{cfortran_8h_ab7123126e4885ef647dd9c6e3807a21c}{s}}[1] = 0.5 * dx\_new + range\_new * \mbox{\hyperlink{cfortran_8h_ab7123126e4885ef647dd9c6e3807a21c}{s}}[1] / range;}
